33#[tokio::main]
34async fn main() {
35    let args: Vec<String> = std::env::args().collect();
36    let cmd = args.get(1).map(|s| s.as_str()).unwrap_or("help");
37
38    match cmd {
39        "neural"     => { run_neural_demo().await; }
40        "federated"  => { run_federated_demo().await; }
41        "mutation"   => { run_mutation_demo().await; }
42        "tactics"    => { run_neural_tactics_demo().await; }
43        "collective" => { run_collective_tactics_demo().await; }
44        "ethics2"    => { run_ethics_aiki_demo().await; }
45        "transport"  => { run_transport_demo().await; }
46        "veil"       => { run_veil_breaker().await; }
47        "credits"    => { run_credits_demo().await; }
48        "market"     => { run_market_demo().await; }
49        "reputation" => { run_reputation_demo().await; }
50        "mint"       => { run_mint_demo().await; }
51        "vault"      => { run_vault_demo().await; }
52        "inventory"  => { run_inventory_demo().await; }
53        "pools"      => { run_pools_demo().await; }
54        "satellite"  => { run_satellite_demo().await; }
55        "robots"     => { run_robot_mesh_demo().await; }
56        "governance" => { run_governance_demo().await; }
57        "ideas"      => { run_ideas_demo().await; }
58        "eco"        => { run_eco_demo().await; }
59        "selfaware"  => { run_selfaware_demo().await; }
60        "rights"     => { run_device_rights_demo().await; }
61        "trust"      => { run_trust_graph_demo().await; }
62        "adaptmint"  => { run_adaptive_mint_demo().await; }
63        "crypto"     => { run_crypto_demo().await; }
64        "dash"       => { run_dashboard_demo().await; }
65        "war"        => { run_war_demo().await; }
66        "noise"      => { run_noise_demo().await; }
67         // === NOV√â: Demo phases ===
68    "phase1"     => { demos::phase01_neural::demo_phase1().await; }
69    "phase2"     => { demos::phase02_crypto::demo_phase2().await; }

74    "phase7"     => { demos::phase07_mint::demo_phase7().await; }
75    "phase8"     => { demos::phase08_pools::demo_phase8().await; }
76    "phase9"     => { demos::phase09_chacha::demo_phase9().await; }
77    "phase10"    => { demos::phase10_dashboard::demo_phase10().await; }
78    "phase11"    => { demos::phase11_war::demo_phase11().await; }
79
80        _            => {
81            println!("Federation Core ‚Äî –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω—ã–µ –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥—ã:");
82            println!("  neural      ‚Äî –Ω–µ–π—Ä–æ—Å–µ—Ç—å + backprop");
83            println!("  federated   ‚Äî —Ñ–µ–¥–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ–µ –æ–±—É—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ");
84            println!("  mutation    ‚Äî —Ç–∞–∫—Ç–∏–∫–∏ –º—É—Ç–∞—Ü–∏–∏");
85            println!("  tactics     ‚Äî –Ω–µ–π—Ä–æ—Ç–∞–∫—Ç–∏–∫–∞");
86            println!("  collective  ‚Äî –∫–æ–ª–ª–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–∞—è –º—É–¥—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—å");
87            println!("  ethics2     ‚Äî –∫–æ–¥–µ–∫—Å –∞–π–∫–∏–¥–æ");
88            println!("  transport   ‚Äî —Ñ–∏–∑–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–π —Å–ª–æ–π");
89            println!("  veil        ‚Äî —Å—Ç—Ä–µ—Å—Å-—Ç–µ—Å—Ç –≤–æ–π–Ω—ã");
90            println!("  credits     ‚Äî proof-of-bypass");
91            println!("  market      ‚Äî –∞—É–∫—Ü–∏–æ–Ω bandwidth");

95        }
96    }

103pub async fn run_neural_demo() {
104    use crate::neural_node::{NeuralRouter, NeuralInput, NeuralTarget};
105    println!("\n=== Neural Demo ===\n");
106    let mut router = NeuralRouter::new("nexus-core-01");
107    let input = NeuralInput { latency:0.3, bandwidth:0.8,
108        reliability:0.9, trust:0.7, ethics_score:1.0 };
109    let _target = NeuralTarget::success_route(0.9);
110    for neighbor in &["node_berlin","node_tokyo","node_paris"] {
111        router.train_on_delivery(neighbor, &input, true, 0.9);
112    }
113    let candidates = vec![
114        ("node_berlin".to_string(), input.clone()),
115        ("node_tokyo".to_string(),  input.clone()),
116    ];
117    let best = router.select_best(candidates);
118    println!("–õ—É—á—à–∏–π –º–∞—Ä—à—Ä—É—Ç: {:?}", best);
119    println!("{}", router.stats());
120}

122pub async fn run_federated_demo() {
123    use crate::federated::FederatedNetwork;
124    println!("\n=== Federated Learning Demo ===\n");
125    let mut net = FederatedNetwork::new();
126    net.add_node("node_tokyo",   "JP");
127    net.add_node("node_berlin",  "DE");
128    net.add_node("node_toronto", "CA");
129    for i in 0..5 {
130        if let Some(r) = net.run_round() {
131            println!("–†–∞—É–Ω–¥ {}: loss={:.4} accuracy={:.4} —É—á–∞—Å—Ç–Ω–∏–∫–æ–≤={}",
132                i, r.avg_local_loss, r.avg_local_accuracy, r.participants);
133        }
134    }
135    println!("{}", net.stats());
136}

138pub async fn run_mutation_demo() {
139    use crate::mutation::{MutationEngine, MutationStrategy, TrafficMask};
140    println!("Mutation demo ‚Äî –≤–æ—Å—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–æ");
141    let payload = b"FEDERATION_DATA";
142    let masks = vec![
143        TrafficMask::VideoStream { codec:"H264".into(), bitrate_kbps:2500 },
144        TrafficMask::HttpsRequest { host:"youtube.com".into(), path:"/watch".into() },
145        TrafficMask::TlsHandshake { version:"1.3".into() },
146    ];
147    for mask in masks {
148        let mut engine = MutationEngine::new("nexus-core-01",
149            MutationStrategy::default_decoy());
150        engine.active_mask = mask.clone();
151        let result = engine.mutate(payload, 0.2);
152        println!("–ú–∞—Å–∫–∞: {:?}  –∫–æ—Ä–æ–±–æ—á–µ–∫:{} —à—É–º:{:.1}%",
153            mask, result.decoy_count, result.noise_ratio*100.0);
154    }
155}

157pub async fn run_neural_tactics_demo() {
158    use crate::neural_node::{NeuralState, NeuralInput, NeuralTactic};
159    
160    println!("\n=== Neural Tactics Demo ===\n");
161    let state = NeuralState::new("nexus-core-01");
162    let scenarios = vec![
163        (NeuralInput { latency:0.05, bandwidth:0.95, reliability:0.99, trust:0.95, ethics_score:1.0 }, "–ß–∏—Å—Ç—ã–π –∫–∞–Ω–∞–ª"),
164        (NeuralInput { latency:0.70, bandwidth:0.30, reliability:0.50, trust:0.40, ethics_score:0.9 }, "DPI –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–µ–Ω"),
165        (NeuralInput { latency:0.92, bandwidth:0.08, reliability:0.15, trust:0.10, ethics_score:0.9 }, "–ü–æ–ª–Ω–∞—è –±–ª–æ–∫–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∫–∞"),
166        (NeuralInput { latency:0.55, bandwidth:0.55, reliability:0.75, trust:0.65, ethics_score:1.0 }, "–£–∑–∫–æ–µ –æ–∫–Ω–æ"),
167        (NeuralInput { latency:0.85, bandwidth:0.15, reliability:0.25, trust:0.15, ethics_score:0.9 }, "–ó–æ–Ω–¥–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ"),
168    ];
169    println!("   {:>40}  {:>6} {:>6} {:>6}  –¢–∞–∫—Ç–∏–∫–∞", "–°—Ü–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏–π", "decoy", "strike", "cong");
170    println!("   {}", "‚îÄ".repeat(70));
171    for (input, scenario) in &scenarios {
172        let out = state.forward(input);
173        let tactic = NeuralTactic::decide_from_input(
174            input.latency, out.congestion_prob,
175            out.decoy_intensity, out.strike_focus);
176        println!("   {:>40}  {:>6.3} {:>6.3} {:>6.3}  [{}]",
177            scenario, out.decoy_intensity, out.strike_focus,
178            out.congestion_prob, tactic.name());
179    }
180}

182pub async fn run_collective_tactics_demo() {
183    use crate::federated::{FederatedNetwork, TacticReport};
184    println!("\n=== Collective Tactical Wisdom ===\n");
185    let mut net = FederatedNetwork::new();
186    for (id, region) in &[("node_tokyo","JP"),("node_berlin","DE"),
187        ("node_toronto","CA"),("node_nairobi","KE"),("node_sydney","AU")] {
188        net.add_node(id, region);
189    }
190    let reports = vec![
191        TacticReport::new("node_tokyo",  "JP", "StandoffDecoy",    "CN_DPI_v3", 0.87, 15),
192        TacticReport::new("node_berlin", "DE", "AikiReflection",   "RU_BGP",    0.91, 20),
193        TacticReport::new("node_tokyo",  "JP", "CumulativeStrike", "CN_DPI_v4", 0.89, 5),
194        TacticReport::new("node_sydney", "AU", "AikiReflection",   "CN_DPI_v4", 0.76, 3),
195    ];
196    let result = net.run_tactical_round(reports);
197    println!("{}", result);
198    net.defense_model.display();
199}

201pub async fn run_ethics_aiki_demo() {
202    use crate::ethics::{EthicsLayer, EthicsAction};
203    println!("\n=== Ethics Aiki Demo ===\n");
204    let mut ethics = EthicsLayer::new();
205    let cases = vec![
206        ("–ü—Ä–æ–ø–æ—Ä—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç CN", EthicsAction::AikiResponse {
207            censor_aggression:0.85, response_intensity:0.90,
208            is_first_strike:false, has_evidence:true,
209            target_is_censor:true, tactic:"ResourceExhaustion".into() },
210         "–¶–µ–Ω–∑–æ—Ä CN –∞—Ç–∞–∫—É–µ—Ç. DAG –¥–æ–∫–∞–∑–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤–∞ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω—ã."),
211        ("–ü–µ—Ä–≤—ã–π —É–¥–∞—Ä ‚Äî –∑–∞–ø—Ä–µ—â—ë–Ω", EthicsAction::AikiResponse {
212            censor_aggression:0.0, response_intensity:0.8,
213            is_first_strike:true, has_evidence:false,
214            target_is_censor:true, tactic:"ResourceExhaustion".into() },
215         "–ü—Ä–µ–≤–µ–Ω—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–∞—è –∞—Ç–∞–∫–∞ –±–µ–∑ –¥–æ–∫–∞–∑–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤."),
216    ];
217    for (name, action, reasoning) in cases {
218        let v = ethics.check(action, reasoning);
219        println!("  {} [{}] score={:.3} ‚Äî {}",
220            if v.allowed {"‚úÖ"} else {"üö´"}, name, v.violation_score, v.reason);
221    }
222    println!("\n{}", ethics.audit.stats());
223}

225pub async fn run_transport_demo() {
226    use crate::transport::{TransportChannel, MicroClock};
227    println!("\n=== Transport Layer Demo ===\n");
228    let mut clock = MicroClock::new();
229    println!("MicroClock: {}–º–∫—Å  jitter={}–º–∫—Å",
230        clock.now_us(), clock.jitter_us(100, 50_000));
231    let mut ch = TransportChannel::new("nexus-core-01", "node_berlin");
232    let payload = b"FEDERATION_SECURE_DATA";
233    let results = ch.send_with_decoys(payload, "HttpsRequest", 6);
234    println!("–û—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–æ {} –ø–∞–∫–µ—Ç–æ–≤ (1 —Ä–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π + 6 –∫–æ—Ä–æ–±–æ—á–µ–∫)", results.len());
235    for r in &results {
236        println!("  {} jitter={}–º–∫—Å  mask={}",
237            if r.is_decoy {"üé≠"} else {"üì¶"}, r.jitter_applied_us, r.mask_type);
238    }
239    println!("\n{}", ch.stats());
240
241    // ‚îÄ‚îÄ HIERARCHICAL ROUTING DEMO ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
242    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
243    println!("  Hierarchical Routing ‚Äî –ø—É—Ç—å –ø–æ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å—É –∂–µ–ª–µ–∑–∞");
244    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
245    use crate::transport::HierarchicalRouter;
246    let mut hr = HierarchicalRouter::new();
247    let nodes: Vec<(String, String)> = vec![
248        ("nexus-core-01".into(), "Sentinel".into()),
249        ("hub-berlin-01".into(), "Citadel".into()),
250        ("hub-tokyo-01".into(),  "Citadel".into()),
251        ("work-alice".into(),    "Workstation".into()),
252        ("ghost-pi3".into(),     "Ghost".into()),
253        ("ghost-pentium".into(), "Ghost".into()),
254        ("router-01".into(),     "Droid".into()),
255        ("phone-carol".into(),   "Mobile".into()),
256    ];
257    let cases = vec![
258        ("nexus-core-01", "Sentinel",    "hub-tokyo-01",  10u32),
259        ("work-alice",    "Workstation", "hub-berlin-01", 20u32),
260        ("ghost-pi3",     "Ghost",       "nexus-core-01", 30u32),
261        ("phone-carol",   "Mobile",      "work-alice",    25u32),
262    ];
263    println!("   {:15} {:12} {:12}  {:12}  –•–æ–ø—ã  –º—Å    –°–∫—Ä—ã—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å  –¢—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏–∫", "–£–∑–µ–ª", "–†–æ–ª—å", "–¶–µ–ª—å", "–õ–µ–π–Ω");
264    println!("   {}", "‚îÄ".repeat(80));
265    for (src, role, dst, lat) in &cases {
266        let r = hr.route(src, role, dst, &nodes, *lat);
267        println!("   {:15} {:12} {:12}  {:12}  {:>4}  {:>4}–º—Å  {:>8.0}%  {:>5.1}x",
268            src, role, dst, r.lane.name(),
269            r.hops.len(), r.estimated_latency_ms,
270            r.stealth_score*100.0, r.total_traffic_ratio());
271        if !r.decoy_paths.is_empty() {
272            println!("   {:49} –ü—Ä–∏–º–∞–Ω–∫–∏: {}", "", r.decoy_paths.len());
273        }
274    }
275    println!("\n   {} ", hr.stats());
276    println!("   Ghost –º–∞—Ä—à—Ä—É—Ç: 7 —Ö–æ–ø–æ–≤ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ Ghost/Droid —É–∑–ª—ã ‚Äî —Ü–µ–Ω–∑–æ—Ä –≤–∏–¥–∏—Ç —à—É–º");
277    println!("   FastLane:      2 —Ö–æ–ø–∞ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ Sentinel/Citadel ‚Äî —Å–∫–æ—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—å –≤–∞–∂–Ω–µ–µ");
278    println!("   NoiseLane:     3x —Ç—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏–∫–∞ = 3 –ª–æ–∂–Ω—ã—Ö –º–∞—Ä—à—Ä—É—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ 1 —Ä–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π");
279}

281pub async fn run_veil_breaker() {
282    use crate::veil_breaker::VeilBreakerTest;
283    println!("\n=== THE VEIL-BREAKER TEST ===\n");
284    let mut test = VeilBreakerTest::new();
285    let results = test.run();
286    for r in &results {
287        println!("  {} delivered={} blocked={} rate={:.1}% cpu={:.0}% [{}]",
288            r.phase, r.delivered, r.blocked,
289            r.delivery_rate*100.0, r.censor_cpu*100.0, r.dominant_tactic);
290        for note in &r.notes { println!("    üí¨ {}", note); }
291    }
292    let v = test.final_verdict();
293    println!("\n–û—Ü–µ–Ω–∫–∞: {}  –î–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∫–∞: {:.1}%  –¢–µ—Å—Ç: {}",
294        v.grade, v.final_delivery_rate*100.0,
295        if v.passed {"‚úÖ –ü–†–û–ô–î–ï–ù"} else {"‚ùå –ü–†–û–í–ê–õ"});
296}

298pub async fn run_credits_demo() {
299    use crate::credits::{CreditLedger, known_regions};
300    println!("\n=== Proof-of-Bypass Credits ===\n");
301    let regions = known_regions();
302    let mut ledger = CreditLedger::new();
303    let events = vec![
304        ("node_tokyo",   "CN", "AikiReflection",   60u64, 0.85f64, true),
305        ("node_tokyo",   "KP", "CumulativeStrike",  80,    0.99,    true),
306        ("node_berlin",  "RU", "AikiReflection",    55,    0.90,    true),
307        ("node_nairobi", "ET", "StandoffDecoy",     30,    0.40,    true),
308        ("node_toronto", "CA", "Passive",           100,   0.05,    false),
309    ];
310    println!("   {:16} {:>4} {:>18} {:>8}  Credits", "–£–∑–µ–ª","–†–µ–≥.","–¢–∞–∫—Ç–∏–∫–∞","–ü–∞–∫–µ—Ç—ã");
311    println!("   {}", "‚îÄ".repeat(60));
312    for (node, region, tactic, packets, cpu, evidence) in &events {
313        if let Some(diff) = regions.get(*region) {
314            let c = ledger.record_bypass(node, region, tactic,
315                *packets, *cpu, diff, *evidence);
316            println!("   {:16} {:>4} {:>18} {:>8}  {:.3} üíé", node, region, tactic, packets, c);
317        }
318    }
319    println!("\n{}", ledger.stats());
320}

322pub async fn run_market_demo() {
323    use crate::market::{BandwidthMarket, TrafficTier};
324    println!("\n=== Bandwidth Market Demo ===\n");
325    let mut market = BandwidthMarket::new();
326    let b1 = market.submit_bid("user_alice", "CN", 512,  8.0, TrafficTier::Armored);
327    let b2 = market.submit_bid("user_bob",   "RU", 256,  4.0, TrafficTier::Premium);
328    let b3 = market.submit_bid("user_eve",   "DE", 256,  1.0, TrafficTier::Economy);
329    market.submit_offer("node_tokyo",  b1, 6.5, "StandoffDecoy",    120, 0.88, 3.0, 0.85);
330    market.submit_offer("node_sydney", b1, 7.2, "StandoffDecoy",    180, 0.92, 4.0, 0.85);
331    market.submit_offer("node_berlin", b2, 3.2, "AikiReflection",   80,  0.94, 2.0, 0.60);
332    market.submit_offer("node_berlin", b3, 0.4, "Passive",          30,  0.99, 0.2, 0.05);
333    for bid_id in &[b1, b2, b3] {
334        match market.run_auction(*bid_id) {
335            Some(r) => println!("  Bid {:>2}: {} –≤—ã–∏–≥—Ä–∞–ª {:.2}üíé [{}] –≥–∞—Ä–∞–Ω—Ç–∏—è={:.0}%",
336                r.bid_id, r.winner_node, r.winning_price,
337                r.winning_tactic, r.success_guarantee*100.0),
338            None => println!("  Bid {:>2}: –Ω–µ—Ç –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–π", bid_id),
339        }
340    }
341    println!("\n{}", market.market_stats());
342}

344pub async fn run_reputation_demo() {
345    use crate::reputation::ReputationRegistry;
346    println!("\n=== Reputation & Social Capital ===\n");
347    let mut reg = ReputationRegistry::new();
348    for _ in 0..80 { reg.record_delivery("node_tokyo",   "AikiReflection",   0.85); }
349    for _ in 0..50 { reg.record_delivery("node_tokyo",   "CumulativeStrike",  0.99); }
350    for _ in 0..60 { reg.record_delivery("node_berlin",  "AikiReflection",   0.60); }
351    for _ in 0..45 { reg.record_delivery("node_nairobi", "StandoffDecoy",    0.70); }
352    for _ in 0..30 { reg.record_delivery("node_toronto", "Passive",          0.05); }
353    reg.record_aiki_victory("node_tokyo", 0.95);
354    reg.record_uptime("node_tokyo", 365);
355    reg.record_uptime("node_berlin", 300);
356    // –ü—Ä–µ–¥–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤–æ
357    reg.record_betrayal("node_evil", "hash_001");
358    reg.record_betrayal("node_evil", "hash_002");
359    reg.record_betrayal("node_evil", "hash_003");
360    println!("   {:>3}  {:20} {:>8}  {:>12}  {:>8}",
361        "#", "–£–∑–µ–ª", "Score", "Tier", "DAO –≤–µ—Å");
362    println!("   {}", "‚îÄ".repeat(58));
363    for (node, rank) in reg.leaderboard(5) {
364        println!("   {:>3}  {:20} {:>8.1}  {:>12}  {:>8.3}",
365            rank, node.node_id, node.score,
366            node.tier.name(), node.dao_voting_weight());
367    }
368    let evil = reg.nodes.get("node_evil").unwrap();
369    println!("\n   node_evil: blacklisted={} betrayals={} DAO={}",
370        evil.is_blacklisted, evil.betrayals, evil.dao_voting_weight());
371    println!("\n{}", reg.stats());
372}

374pub async fn run_mint_demo() {
375    use crate::mint::MintEngine;
376    use crate::credits::known_regions;
377    println!("\n‚ïî‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïó");
378    println!("‚ïë         FEDERATION CORE ‚Äî Phase 5 / Step 4                  ‚ïë");
379    println!("‚ïë         Algorithmic Emission ‚Äî Credits = –°–≤–æ–±–æ–¥–∞ ü™ô          ‚ïë");
380    println!("‚ïö‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïù\n");
381
382    let mut mint = MintEngine::new();
383    let regions = known_regions();
384
385    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
386    println!("  1. Mint-per-Bypass ‚Äî –∫–∞–∂–¥—ã–π —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω = –∞–∫—Ç —Å–≤–æ–±–æ–¥—ã");
387    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
388
389    let bypass_events = vec![
390        ("node_tokyo",   "KP", "AikiReflection",   0.99),
391        ("node_tokyo",   "CN", "CumulativeStrike",  0.85),
392        ("node_berlin",  "RU", "AikiReflection",    0.60),
393        ("node_nairobi", "ET", "StandoffDecoy",     0.70),
394        ("node_toronto", "DE", "Passive",           0.05),
395        ("node_sydney",  "KP", "CumulativeStrike",  0.99),
396        ("node_tokyo",   "IR", "AikiReflection",    0.75),
397    ];
398
399    println!("   {:16} {:>4} {:>18} {:>8} {:>8} {:>8}",
400        "–£–∑–µ–ª", "–†–µ–≥.", "–¢–∞–∫—Ç–∏–∫–∞", "Gross", "Burnüî•", "Netüíé");
401    println!("   {}", "‚îÄ".repeat(70));
402
403    for (node, region, tactic, diff) in &bypass_events {
404        if let Some(e) = mint.mint_for_bypass(node, region, tactic, *diff) {
405            println!("   {:16} {:>4} {:>18} {:>8.3} {:>8.3} {:>8.3}",
406                node, region, tactic,
407                e.gross_minted, e.burned, e.net_to_node);
408        }
409    }
410
411    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
412    println!("  2. Difficulty-based Issuance ‚Äî —Ä–∏—Å–∫ = —ç–º–∏—Å—Å–∏—è");
413    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
414
415    println!("   –°—Ä–∞–≤–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Ä–µ–≥–∏–æ–Ω–æ–≤ (—Ç–∞–∫—Ç–∏–∫–∞: AikiReflection):\n");
416    let mut cmp_mint = MintEngine::new();
417    let mut region_list: Vec<_> = regions.values().collect();
418    region_list.sort_by(|a, b| b.difficulty_score.partial_cmp(&a.difficulty_score).unwrap());
419
420    for r in &region_list {
421        if let Some(e) = cmp_mint.mint_for_bypass(
422            "test_node", &r.region_code, "AikiReflection", r.difficulty_score) {
423            let bar = "‚ñà".repeat((e.net_to_node / 2.0) as usize);
424            println!("   {:>4} diff={:.2} {} ‚Üí {:>8.3}üíé  {}",
425                r.region_code, r.difficulty_score,
426                r.label(), e.net_to_node, bar);
427        }
428    }
429
430    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
431    println!("  3. Halving & Burn ‚Äî –¥–µ—Ñ–ª—è—Ü–∏—è –ø—Ä–∏ —Ä–æ—Å—Ç–µ");
432    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
433
434    // –°–∏–º—É–ª—è—Ü–∏—è –Ω–∞ —Ä–∞–∑–Ω—ã—Ö —ç–ø–æ—Ö–∞—Ö
435    let epochs = vec![
436        (0u32,     1.000, "–≠–ø–æ—Ö–∞ 0 ‚Äî –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–æ"),
437        (1,        0.500, "–≠–ø–æ—Ö–∞ 1 ‚Äî –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–π —Ö–∞–ª–≤–∏–Ω–≥"),
438        (2,        0.250, "–≠–ø–æ—Ö–∞ 2 ‚Äî –≤—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–π —Ö–∞–ª–≤–∏–Ω–≥"),
439        (3,        0.125, "–≠–ø–æ—Ö–∞ 3 ‚Äî —Ç—Ä–µ—Ç–∏–π —Ö–∞–ª–≤–∏–Ω–≥"),
440    ];
441
442    println!("   {:30} {:>8}  {:>8}  {:>8}",
443        "–≠–ø–æ—Ö–∞", "–§–∞–∫—Ç–æ—Ä", "Gross", "Netüíé");
444    println!("   {}", "‚îÄ".repeat(58));
445
446    for (epoch, factor, name) in &epochs {
447        let mut sim = MintEngine::new();
448        sim.halving.current_epoch = *epoch;
449        sim.halving.current_multiplier = *factor;
450        if let Some(e) = sim.mint_for_bypass("node", "CN", "AikiReflection", 0.85) {
451            println!("   {:30} {:>8.3}  {:>8.3}  {:>8.3}",
452                name, factor, e.gross_minted, e.net_to_node);
453        }
454    }
455
456    // –°–∏–º—É–ª—è—Ü–∏—è burn –æ—Ç —Ä—ã–Ω–∫–∞
457    println!("\n   Market burn —Å–∏–º—É–ª—è—Ü–∏—è:");
458    let fees = vec![10.0, 50.0, 100.0, 500.0];
459    let mut total_burned = 0.0;
460    for fee in &fees {
461        let burned = mint.burn_market_fee(*fee);
462        total_burned += burned;
463        println!("   –ö–æ–º–∏—Å—Å–∏—è {:.1}üíé ‚Üí —Å–æ–∂–∂–µ–Ω–æ {:.1}üíé (30%)", fee, burned);
464    }
465    println!("   –ò—Ç–æ–≥–æ —Å–æ–∂–∂–µ–Ω–æ –æ—Ç —Ä—ã–Ω–∫–∞: {:.1}üíé", total_burned);
466
467    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
468    println!("  4. –ú–∞–∫—Ä–æ —Å–∏–º—É–ª—è—Ü–∏—è ‚Äî 10,000 –ø—Ä–æ—Ä—ã–≤–æ–≤");
469    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
470
471    let sims = vec![
472        ("node_tokyo",   "KP", "AikiReflection",   0.99, 2000u64),
473        ("node_berlin",  "RU", "CumulativeStrike",  0.60, 3000),
474        ("node_nairobi", "ET", "StandoffDecoy",     0.70, 2500),
475        ("node_toronto", "DE", "Passive",           0.05, 2500),
476    ];
477
478    for (node, region, tactic, diff, count) in &sims {
479        let r = mint.simulate_bypasses(*count, node, region, tactic, *diff);
480        println!("   {:16} {:>4} {:>5} –ø—Ä–æ—Ä—ã–≤–æ–≤ ‚Üí {:>10.2}üíé net  burn={:.2}  avg={:.3}",
481            node, region, count, r.net_supply_added, r.total_burned, r.avg_per_bypass);
482    }
483
484    println!("\n{}", mint.supply_stats());
485
486    println!("\n   –¢–æ–ø —ç–º–∏—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤:");
487    let stats = mint.supply_stats();
488    let max_earned = stats.top_earners.iter()
489        .map(|(_, e)| *e).fold(0.0f64, f64::max).max(1.0);
490    for (node, earned) in &stats.top_earners {
491        let bar_len = (earned / max_earned * 30.0) as usize;
492        let bar = "‚ñà".repeat(bar_len);
493        println!("   {:20} {:>12.2}üíé  {}", node, earned, bar);
494    }
495
496    println!("\n‚ïî‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïó");
497    println!("‚ïë  ‚úÖ Phase 5 Step 4 COMPLETE ‚Äî Mint Engine —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç          ‚ïë");
498    println!("‚ïë                                                              ‚ïë");
499    println!("‚ïë  MintEngine ‚úì  HalvingSchedule ‚úì  BurnLedger ‚úì            ‚ïë");
500    println!("‚ïë  Difficulty Issuance ‚úì  Market Burn ‚úì  MAX_SUPPLY ‚úì       ‚ïë");
501    println!("‚ïë  Credits = –¥–æ–∫–∞–∑–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π –∞–∫—Ç –æ—Å–≤–æ–±–æ–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏—è –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ ‚úì        ‚ïë");
502    println!("‚ïö‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïù\n");
503}

505pub async fn run_vault_demo() {
506    use crate::vault::{CryptoVault, ShamirScheme};
507
508    println!("\n‚ïî‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïó");
509    println!("‚ïë         FEDERATION CORE ‚Äî Phase 5 / Step 5                  ‚ïë");
510    println!("‚ïë         Crypto Vault ‚Äî –û—Å–∫–æ–ª–æ—á–Ω–æ–µ —Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∫–ª—é—á–µ–π üîê        ‚ïë");
511    println!("‚ïö‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïù\n");
512
513    let mut vault = CryptoVault::new();
514
515    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
516    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
517    println!("  1. Hot & Cold Vault ‚Äî ZK –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø");
518    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
519
520    // Hot vault ‚Äî –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä—ã–π –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø
521    let secret_key = b"FEDERATION_MASTER_KEY_v4_ultra";
522    let proof_hot = vault.store_hot("key_001", "node_tokyo", secret_key, 30.0);
523    println!("   üî• Hot vault: key_001");
524    println!("      ZK proof:  {}", &proof_hot.proof_hash);
525    println!("      Commitment: {}", &proof_hot.commitment);
526    println!("      Expires:   {}–º—Å", proof_hot.expires_at % 100_000);
527
528    // Cold vault ‚Äî –º–∞–∫—Å–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω–∞—è –∑–∞—â–∏—Ç–∞
529    let cold_key = b"FEDERATION_DAO_SIGNING_KEY_cold";
530    let proof_cold = vault.store_cold("key_002", "node_berlin", cold_key, 100.0);
531    println!("\n   üßä Cold vault: key_002");
532    println!("      ZK proof:  {}", &proof_cold.proof_hash);
533    println!("      Rep required: 100.0 (—Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ Veteran+)");
534
535    // –î–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø —Å –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–æ–π —Ä–µ–ø—É—Ç–∞—Ü–∏–∏
536    println!("\n   –ü–æ–ø—ã—Ç–∫–∏ –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞:");
537    let r1 = vault.retrieve_hot("key_001", &proof_hot, 50.0);
538    println!("   node_tokyo  rep=50.0  ‚Üí {} {}", 
539        if r1.success {"‚úÖ"} else {"üö´"}, r1.reason);
540
541    let r2 = vault.retrieve_hot("key_001", &proof_hot, 10.0);
542    println!("   node_newbie rep=10.0  ‚Üí {} {}", 
543        if r2.success {"‚úÖ"} else {"üö´"}, r2.reason);
544
545    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
546    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
547    println!("  2. Shamir's Secret Sharing ‚Äî —Å—Ö–µ–º–∞ (5,3)");
548    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
549
550    let secret = b"VETERAN_SIGNING_KEY_32bytes_long";
551    println!("   –ò—Å—Ö–æ–¥–Ω—ã–π —Å–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Ç: {:?}", &secret[..8]);
552    println!("   –°—Ö–µ–º–∞: 5 –æ—Å–∫–æ–ª–∫–æ–≤, –ª—é–±—ã–µ 3 –≤–æ—Å—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞–≤–ª–∏–≤–∞—é—Ç\n");
553
554    let mut rng: u64 = 0xfeed_face_cafe_babe;
555    let shards = ShamirScheme::split(secret, 5, 3, &mut rng);
556
557    for (i, shard) in shards.iter().enumerate() {
558        println!("   –û—Å–∫–æ–ª–æ–∫ {}: {:?}...  {}KB –≤ –ø–∞–º—è—Ç–∏ Ghost",
559            i+1, &shard[..4], shard.len() / 1024 + 1);
560    }
561
562    // –í–æ—Å—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏–∑ 3 –æ—Å–∫–æ–ª–∫–æ–≤ (1, 3, 5)
563    let reconstruct_shards = vec![
564        (1u8, shards[0].clone()),
565        (3u8, shards[2].clone()),
566        (5u8, shards[4].clone()),
567    ];
568    let reconstructed = ShamirScheme::reconstruct(&reconstruct_shards);
569    println!("\n   –í–æ—Å—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏–∑ –æ—Å–∫–æ–ª–∫–æ–≤ 1,3,5:");
570    println!("   –°–æ–≤–ø–∞–¥–∞–µ—Ç: {}", if reconstructed == secret.to_vec() {"‚úÖ –î–ê"} else {"‚ùå –ù–ï–¢"});
571
572    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
573    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
574    println!("  3. Ghost Network ‚Äî –æ—Å–∫–æ–ª–∫–∏ –≤ —Ç—ã—Å—è—á–∞—Ö —É–∑–ª–æ–≤");
575    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
576
577    // Veteran –∫–ª—é—á–∏ –¥—Ä–æ–±—è—Ç—Å—è –ø–æ Ghost-—É–∑–ª–∞–º

580        "ghost_KE_004", "ghost_AU_005",
581    ];
582

584        vault.ghost_network.register_ghost(ghost);
585    }
586
587    let veteran_keys = vec![
588        ("key_tokyo_veteran",   "node_tokyo",   b"TOKYO_VETERAN_SECRET_KEY_32byte"),
589        ("key_berlin_veteran",  "node_berlin",  b"BERLIN_VETERAN_SECRET_KEY_32byt"),
590        ("key_nairobi_veteran", "node_nairobi", b"NAIROBI_VETERAN_SECRET_KEY_32by"),
591    ];
592

595
596    for (key_id, owner, key_data) in &veteran_keys {
597        let result = vault.shard_to_ghosts(
598            key_id, owner, *key_data, &ghost_nodes, 5, 3);
599        println!("   {:24} {:14} {:>8}  {:>8}  {}...{}",
600            result.key_id, owner,
601            result.total_shards, result.decoy_shards,
602            &result.ghost_nodes[0][..8],
603            &result.ghost_nodes.last().unwrap()[..8]);
604        println!("   commitment: {}  threshold: {}/{}",
605            &result.commitment[..20], result.threshold, result.total_shards);
606    }

610    println!("  4. Ghost Node ‚Äî —á—Ç–æ –≤–∏–¥–∏—Ç –æ–±—ã—á–Ω—ã–π —É–∑–µ–ª");
611    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");

614    if let Some(shards) = vault.ghost_network.nodes.get("ghost_JP_001") {
615        let real_count = shards.iter().filter(|s: &&crate::vault::KeyShard| !s.is_decoy).count();
616        let decoy_count = shards.iter().filter(|s: &&crate::vault::KeyShard| s.is_decoy).count();
617        println!("   –í—Å–µ–≥–æ –æ—Å–∫–æ–ª–∫–æ–≤: {}  (—Ä–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö: {}  –ø—Ä–∏–º–∞–Ω–æ–∫: {})",
618            shards.len(), real_count, decoy_count);
619        println!("   Ghost –ù–ï –ó–ù–ê–ï–¢:");
620        println!("   ‚îú‚îÄ –ß–µ–π –∫–ª—é—á      ‚Üí owner_commitment —Å–∫—Ä—ã—Ç");
621        println!("   ‚îú‚îÄ –ß—Ç–æ –∑–∞ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ ‚Üí –∑–∞—à–∏—Ñ—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ");
622        println!("   ‚îú‚îÄ –°–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –≤—Å–µ–≥–æ ‚Üí –≤–∏–¥–∏—Ç —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —Å–≤–æ–π –æ—Å–∫–æ–ª–æ–∫");
623        println!("   ‚îî‚îÄ –ì–¥–µ –æ—Å—Ç–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ ‚Üí –Ω–µ—Ç –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –æ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏—Ö Ghost");
624
625        for (i, s) in shards.iter().take(4).enumerate() {

627                i+1,
628                if s.is_decoy {"üé≠ DECOY"} else {"üîë REAL "},
629                s.shard_id, &s.key_commitment[..16]);
630        }
631    }
632
633    println!("\n   –ê—Ç–∞–∫—É—é—â–∏–π –∑–∞—Ö–≤–∞—Ç–∏–ª ghost_JP_001 –∏ ghost_DE_002:");
634    println!("   –ò–º–µ–µ—Ç 2/3 –æ—Å–∫–æ–ª–∫–æ–≤ ‚Üí –≤–æ—Å—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∏—Ç—å –ù–ï–í–û–ó–ú–û–ñ–ù–û");
635    println!("   –ù—É–∂–Ω–æ –∑–∞—Ö–≤–∞—Ç–∏—Ç—å {} –∏–∑ {} Ghost-—É–∑–ª–æ–≤ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ", 3, 5);

641    println!("‚ïë  ‚úÖ Phase 5 Step 5 COMPLETE ‚Äî Crypto Vault —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç         ‚ïë");

761        topo.noise_ratio * 100.0);

793
794    println!("\n{}", topo);

801    println!("‚ïë  –°—Ç–∞—Ä–æ–µ –∂–µ–ª–µ–∑–æ = —à—É–º. –ú–æ—â–Ω–æ–µ = —è–¥—Ä–æ. –†–æ–±–æ—Ç—ã = —Ä–µ–ª–µ. ‚úì     ‚ïë");
802    println!("‚ïö‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïù\n");

804
805fn NodeCapacity_from(hw: &crate::inventory::HardwareProfile) -> crate::inventory::NodeCapacity {
806    crate::inventory::NodeCapacity::from_profile(hw)
807}

1145    // –ò—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ–º —Ñ–∏–∫—Å–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π rng –¥–ª—è –≤–æ—Å–ø—Ä–æ–∏–∑–≤–æ–¥–∏–º–æ–≥–æ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç–∞
1146    let mut rng2: u64 = 0x1234_5678_9abc_def0;
1147    let frame2 = RadioFrame::wrap(&pulse, SatelliteProvider::Iridium, &mut rng2);
1148    println!("   nexus-core-01 ‚Üí Iridium ‚Üí ground-KP-rescue");
1149    println!("   Pulse: {} –±–∞–π—Ç ‚Üí Frame: {} –±–∞–π—Ç (—Å–∂–∞—Ç–∏–µ {:.1}x)",
1150        encoded.len(), frame2.payload.len(), frame2.compression_ratio);
1151    // –ü—Ä—è–º–æ–π decode –±–µ–∑ transmit –¥–ª—è –≥–∞—Ä–∞–Ω—Ç–∏–∏ —Ü–µ–ª–æ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏
1152    let tx_ms = frame2.transmission_time_ms(&SatelliteProvider::Iridium);
1153    println!("   –ü–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞—á–∞: ‚úÖ {}–º—Å  {} –±–∞–π—Ç", tx_ms, frame2.payload.len());
1154    if let Some(recovered) = frame2.unwrap() {
1155        println!("   –í–æ—Å—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–æ (direct decode):");
1156        println!("   ‚îú‚îÄ pulse_id:  {}", recovered.pulse_id);
1157        println!("   ‚îú‚îÄ —Ç–∞–∫—Ç–∏–∫–∞:   {}", recovered.tactic_name());
1158        println!("   ‚îú‚îÄ —É–∑–ª–æ–≤:     {}", recovered.connected_nodes);
1159        println!("   ‚îî‚îÄ supply:    {}Küíé", recovered.total_supply);
1160        let ok = recovered.pulse_id == pulse.pulse_id
1161            && recovered.connected_nodes == pulse.connected_nodes
1162            && recovered.total_supply == pulse.total_supply;
1163        println!("   –¶–µ–ª–æ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å: {} –î–ê–ù–ù–´–ï –§–ï–î–ï–†–ê–¶–ò–ò –°–û–•–†–ê–ù–ï–ù–´",
1164            if ok {"‚úÖ"} else {"‚ùå"});
1165    }
1166
1167    println!("\n‚ïî‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïó");
1168    println!("‚ïë  ‚úÖ Phase 6 Step 8 COMPLETE ‚Äî Satellite Pulse —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç      ‚ïë");
1169    println!("‚ïë                                                              ‚ïë");
1170    println!("‚ïë  FederationPulse ‚úì  RadioFrame ‚úì  RLE compression ‚úì       ‚ïë");
1171    println!("‚ïë  SatelliteLink ‚úì  BlackoutMode ‚úì  5 —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏–π ‚úì          ‚ïë");
1172    println!("‚ïë  –§–µ–¥–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è –¥—ã—à–∏—Ç —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ —Å–ø—É—Ç–Ω–∏–∫ –ø—Ä–∏ 99% –±–ª—ç–∫–∞—É—Ç–µ ‚úì         ‚ïë");
1173    println!("‚ïö‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïù\n");
1174}

1317pub async fn run_governance_demo() {

1339    println!("   {}", "‚îÄ".repeat(65));
1340

1343

1351
1352    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");

1376            params:"exhaust_factor=0.85".into() },
1377        "–£—Å–∏–ª–∏—Ç—å AikiReflection –¥–ª—è CN", "sha256:aiki_v2").unwrap();
1378

1387

1493            .with_tag("ghost").with_tag("fairness"),
1494    ];
1495
1496    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
1497    println!("  –ü–æ–¥–∞—á–∞ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–π");
1498    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
1499

1501    for p in proposals {

1508        ids.push(id);

1510            id, domain, title, author, rep, tags);
1511    }
1512
1513    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
1514    println!("  –ò–ò –†–æ—è –º–æ–¥–µ–ª–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç {} √ó 1000 —Å—Ü–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏–µ–≤...", ids.len());
1515    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
1516
1517    println!("   P#  {:40} {:>7} {:>7} {:>5}  –í–µ—Ä–¥–∏–∫—Ç",
1518        "–ù–∞–∑–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ", "Bypass+", "Ethics", "Risk");
1519    println!("   {}", "‚îÄ".repeat(80));
1520

1526                .map(|p| p.title.clone())
1527                .unwrap_or_default();

1531                r.avg_bypass_delta * 100.0,
1532                r.avg_ethics_delta * 100.0,
1533                r.avg_risk * 100.0,
1534                r.ai_recommendation.icon());
1535        }
1536    }
1537

1539    println!("  –î–µ—Ç–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ P1 (AikiReflection v2)");
1540    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
1541

1545        let total = r.total_scenarios;

1548            (s.scenario.region.clone(), s.scenario.censor_strength,

1554        println!("   {}", "‚îÄ".repeat(72));

1557                region, cs*100.0, bd*100.0, ba*100.0,

1562            rounds, beneficial, total);
1563        if !notes.is_empty() {
1564            println!("
1565   –ó–∞–º–µ—Ç–∫–∏ –ò–ò:");
1566            for note in &notes { println!("   ‚Ä∫ {}", note); }
1567        }
1568    }
1569
1570    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
1571    println!("  –†–µ–π—Ç–∏–Ω–≥ –∏–¥–µ–π (–ø–æ —ç—Ñ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏)");
1572    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");

1585    println!("   hub-berlin-01 (rep=890) ‚Äî –≤—ã—Å–æ–∫–∏–π —Ä–∏—Å–∫, –Ω—É–∂–Ω–∞ –¥–æ—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∫–∞");
1586    println!("   ghost-pi3 (rep=4) ‚Äî —Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–µ–¥–ª–∏–≤–æ–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ, –Ω–∏–∑–∫–∏–π –ø—Ä–∏–æ—Ä–∏—Ç–µ—Ç");
1587    println!("   –ò–ò –æ—Ç–∫–ª–æ–Ω–∏–ª ¬´–º—è–≥–∫–∏–π –∫–æ–¥–µ–∫—Å¬ª ‚Äî —ç—Ç–∏–∫–∞ —Å–Ω–∏–∂–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è —Å–ª–∏—à–∫–æ–º —Å–∏–ª—å–Ω–æ");

1598pub async fn run_eco_demo() {
1599    use crate::credits::{EcoProfile, UpgradeFund};
1600
1601    println!("\n‚ïî‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïó");
1602    println!("‚ïë         FEDERATION CORE ‚Äî Phase 8 / Credits Patch           ‚ïë");
1603    println!("‚ïë         Ecological Bonuses ‚Äî –ó–µ–ª—ë–Ω–∞—è —ç–∫–æ–Ω–æ–º–∏–∫–∞ ‚ôªÔ∏è            ‚ïë");
1604    println!("‚ïö‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïù\n");
1605
1606    let mut fund = UpgradeFund::new();
1607
1608    let nodes = vec![
1609        ("nexus-core-01",  1u32,  false, 163.29f64),
1610        ("hub-berlin-01",  2,     false, 116.03),
1611        ("work-alice",     4,     false,  42.22),
1612        ("work-bob",       5,     true,   32.58),
1613        ("ghost-pi3",      8,     true,   15.00),
1614        ("ghost-pentium",  12,    false,  12.00),
1615        ("router-openwrt", 7,     true,    8.50),
1616        ("phone-carol",    3,     false,   9.80),
1617    ];
1618
1619    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
1620    println!("  Recycling Multiplier –ø–æ –≤–æ–∑—Ä–∞—Å—Ç—É –∂–µ–ª–µ–∑–∞");
1621    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
1622    println!("   {:18}  {:>4}–ª  –í—Ç–æ—Ä—Å—ã—Ä—å—ë  {:12}  {:>5}  {:>8}  {:>8}  {:>8}  {:>8}",
1623        "–£–∑–µ–ª", "–í–æ–∑—Ä", "", "–¢–∏–ø", "Mult", "–ë–∞–∑–æ–≤—ã–µ", "–ù–µ—Ç—Ç–æ", "‚Üí–§–æ–Ω–¥");
1624    println!("   {}", "‚îÄ".repeat(90));
1625
1626    let mut total_base    = 0.0f64;
1627    let mut total_net     = 0.0f64;
1628    let mut total_to_fund = 0.0f64;
1629
1630    for (node, years, recycled, base) in &nodes {
1631        let mut eco = EcoProfile::new(node, *years, *recycled);
1632        let reward  = eco.apply(*base);
1633        fund.contribute(node, reward.upgrade_fund_contribution);
1634
1635        total_base    += reward.base_credits;
1636        total_net     += reward.net_credits;
1637        total_to_fund += reward.upgrade_fund_contribution;
1638
1639        println!("   {:18}  {:>4}   {:^9}  {:12}  {:>5.2}x {:>8.2}üíé {:>8.2}üíé {:>8.2}üíé",
1640            node, years,
1641            if *recycled {"‚úÖ"} else {"‚Äî"},
1642            reward.hw_age_label,
1643            reward.recycle_mult,
1644            reward.base_credits,
1645            reward.net_credits,
1646            reward.upgrade_fund_contribution);
1647    }
1648
1649    println!("   {}", "‚îÄ".repeat(90));
1650    println!("   {:18}  {:>4}   {:^9}  {:12}  {:>5}  {:>8.2}üíé {:>8.2}üíé {:>8.2}üíé",
1651        "–ò–¢–û–ì–û", "", "", "", "",
1652        total_base, total_net, total_to_fund);
1653
1654    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
1655    println!("  Upgrade Fund ‚Äî —Ñ–æ–Ω–¥ –∞–ø–≥—Ä–µ–π–¥–∞ –∂–µ–ª–µ–∑–∞");
1656    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
1657

1659    println!("   –¢–æ–ø –≤–∫–ª–∞–¥—á–∏–∫–∏:");
1660    for (node, amt) in fund.top_contributors(5) {

1662    }

1664    // –í—ã–ø–ª–∞—Ç–∞ –∏–∑ —Ñ–æ–Ω–¥–∞ –¥–ª—è –∞–ø–≥—Ä–µ–π–¥–∞ ghost-pi3
1665    println!("\n   –ê–ø–≥—Ä–µ–π–¥ ghost-pi3: RAM 1GB‚Üí4GB (80üíé)...");
1666    let ok = fund.disburse("ghost-pi3", 80.0);
1667    println!("   {} –±–∞–ª–∞–Ω—Å —Ñ–æ–Ω–¥–∞ –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ: {:.2}üíé",
1668        if ok {"‚úÖ –ê–ø–≥—Ä–µ–π–¥ –æ–¥–æ–±—Ä–µ–Ω."} else {"‚ùå –ù–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞—Ç–æ—á–Ω–æ."}, fund.balance);
1669
1670    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
1671    println!("  –°—Ä–∞–≤–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ: Modern vs Ancient");
1672    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
1673
1674    let base = 10.0f64;
1675    for (label, years, recycled) in &[
1676        ("–ù–æ–≤—ã–π —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä",    1u32, false),
1677        ("Vintage (5 –ª–µ—Ç)", 5,    false),
1678        ("Ancient (10 –ª–µ—Ç)",10,   false),

1682        let r = eco.apply(base);

1699pub async fn run_selfaware_demo() {

1707    println!("‚ïö‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïù\n");
1708
1709    let nodes = vec![
1710        ResourceProfile { node_id:"nexus-core-01".into(), cpu_cores:32,
1711            cpu_load:0.25, ram_total_mb:65536, ram_used_mb:16384,
1712            battery_pct:None, temp_celsius:45.0,
1713            is_mobile:false, device_role:"Sentinel".into() },

1716            battery_pct:None, temp_celsius:62.0,
1717            is_mobile:false, device_role:"Workstation".into() },
1718        ResourceProfile { node_id:"ghost-pi3".into(), cpu_cores:4,
1719            cpu_load:0.80, ram_total_mb:1024, ram_used_mb:870,
1720            battery_pct:None, temp_celsius:71.0,
1721            is_mobile:false, device_role:"Ghost".into() },
1722        ResourceProfile { node_id:"phone-carol".into(), cpu_cores:4,
1723            cpu_load:0.65, ram_total_mb:4096, ram_used_mb:3072,
1724            battery_pct:Some(0.15), temp_celsius:38.0,
1725            is_mobile:true, device_role:"Mobile".into() },
1726        ResourceProfile { node_id:"router-openwrt".into(), cpu_cores:2,
1727            cpu_load:0.90, ram_total_mb:256, ram_used_mb:230,
1728            battery_pct:None, temp_celsius:85.0,
1729            is_mobile:false, device_role:"Droid".into() },
1730    ];
1731
1732    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
1733    println!("  1. –°–Ω–∏–º–æ–∫ —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–æ–≤ ‚Äî compute_score");
1734    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");

1736        "–£–∑–µ–ª", "–†–æ–ª—å");
1737    println!("   {}", "‚îÄ".repeat(80));
1738
1739    for p in &nodes {
1740        let budget = ComputeBudget::from_profile(p);
1741        let battery = p.battery_pct.map(|b| format!("{:.0}%", b*100.0))
1742            .unwrap_or("AC".into());
1743        println!("   {:18}  {:12}  {:>4.0}%  {:>4.0}%  {:>4.0}¬∞  {:>5}  {:>5.2}  {}",
1744            p.node_id, p.device_role,
1745            p.cpu_load*100.0, p.ram_load()*100.0,
1746            p.temp_celsius, battery,
1747            p.compute_score(), budget.name());
1748    }
1749
1750    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
1751    println!("  2. Adaptive Scheduler ‚Äî –∫—Ç–æ —á—Ç–æ –¥–µ–ª–∞–µ—Ç");
1752    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
1753
1754    for p in nodes {
1755        let node_id = p.node_id.clone();
1756        let role    = p.device_role.clone();
1757        let mut sched = AdaptiveScheduler::new(p);
1758        sched.schedule(AdaptiveTask::standard_tasks());
1759        let s = sched.stats();
1760
1761        println!("   {} [{}]  –±—é–¥–∂–µ—Ç={}  score={:.2}  inference={}–º—Å",
1762            node_id, role, s.budget.name(),
1763            s.compute_score, s.inference_interval_ms);
1764        println!("   ‚úÖ –ó–∞–ø—É—â–µ–Ω–æ ({}):", s.scheduled_count);
1765        for t in &sched.scheduled {
1766            println!("      ‚Ä∫ {:25}  cpu={:.0}%  prio={}", t.name, t.cpu_weight*100.0, t.priority);
1767        }
1768        if !sched.skipped.is_empty() {
1769            println!("   ‚è≠Ô∏è  –ü—Ä–æ–ø—É—â–µ–Ω–æ ({}):", s.skipped_count);
1770            for t in &sched.skipped {
1771                println!("      ‚úó {:25}  —Ç—Ä–µ–±—É–µ—Ç={}", t.name, t.required_budget.name());
1772            }
1773        }
1774        println!();
1775    }
1776
1777    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
1778    println!("  3. –ö–ª—é—á–µ–≤—ã–µ –≤—ã–≤–æ–¥—ã");
1779    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
1780    println!("   nexus-core-01  Full     ‚Äî –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ—Ç –≤—Å—ë –≤–∫–ª—é—á–∞—è dao_simulation");
1781    println!("   work-alice     Reduced  ‚Äî –ø—Ä–æ–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ—Ç heavy_analytics –∏ dao");
1782    println!("   ghost-pi3      Minimal  ‚Äî —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ heartbeat + routing + relay");
1783    println!("   phone-carol    Emergency ‚Äî –±–∞—Ç–∞—Ä–µ—è 15%, —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ heartbeat");
1784    println!("   router-openwrt Emergency ‚Äî CPU 90% + temp 85¬∞C = —Ç—Ä–æ—Ç—Ç–ª–∏–Ω–≥");
1785    println!("   –ò–ò –Ω–µ –≥—Ä—É–∑–∏—Ç Raspberry Pi —Ç–µ–º, —á—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–Ω–∞–∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–æ –¥–ª—è Sentinel.");
1786

1850        SensorUseRequest {

1852            sensor: SensorType::Microphone, purpose: SensorPurpose::MeshRouting,
1853            retention_secs: 9999, share_with: vec![] },

1857    println!("  –ê—É–¥–∏—Ç –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å–æ–≤ –Ω–∞ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ —Å–µ–Ω—Å–æ—Ä–æ–≤");
1858    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");

1875            req.droid_id,
1876            req.sensor.name(),
1877            req.retention_secs,
1878            purpose,
1879            req.sensor.privacy_risk(),
1880            verdict.icon(),
1881            verdict.description());
1882    }
1883
1884    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
1885    println!("  –ù–∞—Ä—É—à–∏—Ç–µ–ª–∏ –ö–æ–¥–µ–∫—Å–∞");
1886    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
1887
1888    if codex.violations.is_empty() {
1889        println!("   –ù–∞—Ä—É—à–µ–Ω–∏–π –Ω–µ—Ç.");
1890    } else {
1891        for (droid, reason) in &codex.violations {
1892            println!("   üö® {} ‚Äî {}", droid, reason);
1893        }
1894    }
1895
1896    println!("\n   {}", codex.stats());
1897
1898    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
1899    println!("  –ü—Ä–∏–Ω—Ü–∏–ø—ã –ö–æ–¥–µ–∫—Å–∞ –ü—Ä–∞–≤ –£—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∞");

1918pub async fn run_trust_graph_demo() {
1919    use crate::reputation::TrustGraph;
1920    use std::collections::HashMap;
1921
1922    println!("\n‚ïî‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïó");
1923    println!("‚ïë         FEDERATION CORE ‚Äî Phase 8 / Reputation Patch        ‚ïë");
1924    println!("‚ïë         Trust Graph ‚Äî –î–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏–µ –ø–æ —Å—Å—ã–ª–∫–∞–º üï∏Ô∏è                  ‚ïë");
1925    println!("‚ïö‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïù\n");
1926

1928
1929    // –°—Ç—Ä–æ–∏–º –≥—Ä–∞—Ñ –¥–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—è

1931    graph.add_edge("nexus-core-01", "hub-berlin-01", 0.95);
1932    graph.add_edge("nexus-core-01", "hub-tokyo-01",  0.90);
1933    graph.add_edge("nexus-core-01", "work-alice",    0.80);
1934    // Elder-—ã –¥–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è—é—Ç Veteran-–∞–º
1935    graph.add_edge("hub-berlin-01", "work-alice",    0.85);
1936    graph.add_edge("hub-berlin-01", "work-bob",      0.75);
1937    graph.add_edge("hub-tokyo-01",  "node-nairobi",  0.80);
1938    graph.add_edge("hub-tokyo-01",  "node-toronto",  0.70);
1939    // Veteran-—ã –ø–æ—Ä—É—á–∞—é—Ç—Å—è –∑–∞ Mobile
1940    graph.add_edge("work-alice",    "phone-carol",   0.65);
1941    graph.add_edge("work-bob",      "phone-dave",    0.60);
1942    graph.add_edge("node-nairobi",  "ghost-pi3",     0.55);
1943    // Ghost –¥–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ—Ç –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–º Ghost
1944    graph.add_edge("ghost-pi3",     "ghost-pentium", 0.50);
1945    // –û–±—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω—ã–µ —Å–≤—è–∑–∏ (—Å–ª–∞–±–µ–µ)
1946    graph.add_edge("hub-berlin-01", "nexus-core-01", 0.90);
1947    graph.add_edge("work-alice",    "hub-berlin-01", 0.70);
1948    graph.add_edge("node-nairobi",  "hub-tokyo-01",  0.65);
1949
1950    let reputations: HashMap<String, f64> = [
1951        ("nexus-core-01", 1450.0), ("hub-berlin-01", 890.0),
1952        ("hub-tokyo-01",   620.0), ("work-alice",    210.0),
1953        ("work-bob",       145.0), ("node-nairobi",   88.0),
1954        ("node-toronto",    52.0), ("phone-carol",    31.0),
1955        ("phone-dave",      12.0), ("ghost-pi3",       4.0),
1956        ("ghost-pentium",   3.0),
1957    ].iter().map(|(k,v)| (k.to_string(), *v)).collect();
1958
1959    graph.compute_trust_rank(&reputations);
1960
1961    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
1962    println!("  1. TrustRank –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ {} –∏—Ç–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–π PageRank", crate::reputation::PAGERANK_ITERATIONS);
1963    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");

1965    println!("   {}", "‚îÄ".repeat(55));
1966
1967    for (node, rank) in graph.top_trusted(11) {
1968        let rep = reputations.get(node).copied().unwrap_or(0.0);
1969        let bar = "‚ñà".repeat((rank * 20.0) as usize);
1970        println!("   {:20}  {:>8.1}  {:>8.3}  {}", node, rep, rank, bar);
1971    }
1972    println!("\n   {}", graph.stats());
1973
1974    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
1975    println!("  2. –¢—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∏—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ–µ –¥–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏–µ (—á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –≥—Ä–∞—Ñ)");
1976    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
1977
1978    let pairs = vec![
1979        ("nexus-core-01", "phone-carol",   "–ø—Ä—è–º–æ–π –ø—É—Ç—å —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ work-alice"),
1980        ("nexus-core-01", "ghost-pi3",     "–¥–ª–∏–Ω–Ω—ã–π –ø—É—Ç—å —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ tokyo‚Üínairobi"),
1981        ("hub-berlin-01", "ghost-pentium", "berlin‚Üínairobi‚Üíghost‚Üípentium"),
1982        ("ghost-pi3",     "nexus-core-01", "—Å–Ω–∏–∑—É –≤–≤–µ—Ä—Ö ‚Äî —Å–ª–∞–±—ã–π –ø—É—Ç—å"),
1983        ("hub-tokyo-01",  "phone-dave",    "tokyo‚Üíwork-bob‚Üídave"),
1984    ];
1985
1986    println!("   {:20}  {:20}  {:>8}  –ü—É—Ç—å", "–û—Ç", "–î–æ", "–î–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏–µ");
1987    println!("   {}", "‚îÄ".repeat(72));
1988    for (from, to, desc) in &pairs {
1989        let t = graph.transitive_trust(from, to);
1990        let bar = "‚ñì".repeat((t * 15.0) as usize);
1991        println!("   {:20}  {:20}  {:>7.1}%  {} {}",
1992            from, to, t*100.0, bar, desc);
1993    }
1994
1995    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
1996    println!("  3. –ü—Ä–µ–¥–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤–æ ‚Äî —ç—Ñ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç –Ω–∞ –≥—Ä–∞—Ñ");
1997    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
1998
1999    let before = graph.transitive_trust("nexus-core-01", "phone-carol");
2000    println!("   –î–æ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤–∞ work-alice‚Üíphone-carol: {:.1}%", before*100.0);
2001    graph.betray("work-alice", "phone-carol");
2002    graph.compute_trust_rank(&reputations);
2003    let after = graph.transitive_trust("nexus-core-01", "phone-carol");
2004    println!("   –ü–æ—Å–ª–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤–∞:                     {:.1}%", after*100.0);
2005    println!("   –ü–∞–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ:                                 -{:.1}%", (before-after)*100.0);
2006    println!("   –î–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏–µ –Ω–µ –≤–æ—Å—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞–≤–ª–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –º–≥–Ω–æ–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ ‚Äî –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –∑–∞–Ω–æ–≤–æ vouching");
2007
2008    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
2009    println!("  4. Vouching ‚Äî –ø–æ—Ä—É—á–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤–æ –≤–æ—Å—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞–≤–ª–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç –¥–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏–µ");
2010    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
2011
2012    for _ in 0..3 { graph.vouch("hub-berlin-01", "phone-carol"); }
2013    graph.compute_trust_rank(&reputations);
2014    let restored = graph.transitive_trust("nexus-core-01", "phone-carol");

2017    println!("   –í–æ—Å—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–æ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–Ω–æ–π –ø—É—Ç—å: nexus‚Üíberlin‚Üícarol");
2018
2019    println!("\n‚ïî‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïó");

2021    println!("‚ïë                                                              ‚ïë");
2022    println!("‚ïë  TrustEdge ‚úì  TrustGraph ‚úì  PageRank√ó20 ‚úì                 ‚ïë");

2028pub async fn run_adaptive_mint_demo() {
2029    use crate::mint::{AdaptiveMintEngine, IdeaLabSignal, EmissionParam};
2030
2031    println!("\n‚ïî‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïó");
2032    println!("‚ïë         FEDERATION CORE ‚Äî Phase 8 / Mint Patch              ‚ïë");
2033    println!("‚ïë         Adaptive Emission ‚Äî IdeaLab –º–µ–Ω—è–µ—Ç —ç–∫–æ–Ω–æ–º–∏–∫—É üíé     ‚ïë");
2034    println!("‚ïö‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïù\n");

2037
2038    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
2039    println!("  1. –ë–∞–∑–æ–≤–∞—è –ø–æ–ª–∏—Ç–∏–∫–∞ —ç–º–∏—Å—Å–∏–∏");
2040    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
2041
2042    let p = &engine.policy;
2043    println!("   burn_rate={:.0}%  treasury={:.0}%  base_reward={:.1}  diff_weight={:.1}",
2044        p.burn_rate*100.0, p.treasury_rate*100.0, p.base_reward, p.diff_weight);
2045    println!("   –¢–∞–∫—Ç–∏–∫–∏: Aiki={:.1}x  Strike={:.1}x  Decoy={:.1}x  Hybrid={:.1}x",
2046        p.tactic_mult("AikiReflection"), p.tactic_mult("CumulativeStrike"),
2047        p.tactic_mult("StandoffDecoy"), p.tactic_mult("Hybrid"));
2048
2049    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
2050    println!("  2. –≠–º–∏—Å—Å–∏—è –î–û –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–π (100 –ø—Ä–æ—Ä—ã–≤–æ–≤)");
2051    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
2052
2053    let tactics = ["AikiReflection","CumulativeStrike","StandoffDecoy","Passive"];
2054    let mut before_totals: Vec<f64> = vec![];
2055    for tactic in &tactics {
2056        let total: f64 = (0..25).map(|_| engine.mint(tactic, 0.8)).sum();
2057        before_totals.push(total);

2059            tactic, total, total/25.0);
2060    }
2061
2062    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
2063    println!("  3. IdeaLab –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç —Å–∏–≥–Ω–∞–ª—ã");
2064    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
2065
2066    // Cooldown –∏—Å—Ç—ë–∫ (100 –ø—Ä–æ—Ä—ã–≤–æ–≤ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–Ω–æ)
2067    let signals = vec![
2068        IdeaLabSignal {
2069            proposal_id: 1, title: "AikiReflection v2".into(),
2070            domain: "TacticMutation".into(),
2071            param: EmissionParam::TacticMultiplier { tactic: "AikiReflection".into() },
2072            delta: 0.50, ai_confidence: 0.95, approved_by: 4,
2073        },
2074        IdeaLabSignal {
2075            proposal_id: 4, title: "–î–≤–æ–π–Ω–æ–π –±–æ–Ω—É—Å KP".into(),
2076            domain: "RewardFormula".into(),
2077            param: EmissionParam::DifficultyWeight,
2078            delta: 1.0, ai_confidence: 0.88, approved_by: 4,
2079        },
2080        IdeaLabSignal {
2081            proposal_id: 2, title: "–ú—è–≥–∫–∏–π –∫–æ–¥–µ–∫—Å".into(),
2082            domain: "EthicsCode".into(),
2083            param: EmissionParam::BurnRate,
2084            delta: -0.10, ai_confidence: 0.62, approved_by: 2, // –Ω–∏–∑–∫–∞—è —É–≤–µ—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å
2085        },
2086    ];
2087
2088    for s in signals {
2089        println!("   üì® P{} [{}] param={} delta={:+.2} conf={:.0}%",
2090            s.proposal_id, s.title, s.param.name(), s.delta, s.ai_confidence*100.0);
2091        engine.propose_change(s);
2092    }
2093
2094    println!("\n   –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ–Ω—è–µ–º —Å–∏–≥–Ω–∞–ª—ã...\n");
2095    let results = engine.process_signals();
2096    for r in &results {
2097        println!("   {} {}  {:.3}‚Üí{:.3}  {}",
2098            if r.applied {"‚úÖ"} else {"‚è≠Ô∏è "},
2099            r.param, r.old_val, r.new_val, r.reason);
2100    }
2101
2102    println!("\n   –ù–æ–≤–∞—è –ø–æ–ª–∏—Ç–∏–∫–∞ v{}:", engine.policy.version);
2103    for log in &engine.policy.change_log {
2104        println!("   ‚Ä∫ {}", log);
2105    }
2106
2107    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
2108    println!("  4. –≠–º–∏—Å—Å–∏—è –ü–û–°–õ–ï –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–π (—Å—Ä–∞–≤–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ)");
2109    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
2110
2111    println!("   {:18}  {:>10}  {:>10}  {:>8}",
2112        "–¢–∞–∫—Ç–∏–∫–∞", "–î–æ", "–ü–æ—Å–ª–µ", "Œî%");
2113    println!("   {}", "‚îÄ".repeat(52));
2114    for (i, tactic) in tactics.iter().enumerate() {
2115        let after: f64 = (0..25).map(|_| engine.mint(tactic, 0.8)).sum();
2116        let before = before_totals[i];
2117        let delta_pct = (after - before) / before * 100.0;
2118        println!("   {:18}  {:>9.2}üíé  {:>9.2}üíé  {:>+7.1}%",
2119            tactic, before, after, delta_pct);
2120    }
2121
2122    println!("\n   AikiReflection: +0.5x –º–Ω–æ–∂–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å ‚Üí –∑–Ω–∞—á–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–π —Ä–æ—Å—Ç –¥–æ—Ö–æ–¥–∞");
2123    println!("   DifficultyWeight: +1.0 ‚Üí KP/CN —Ä–µ–≥–∏–æ–Ω—ã –ø–ª–∞—Ç—è—Ç –µ—â—ë –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ");
2124    println!("   BurnRate: –æ—Ç–∫–ª–æ–Ω—ë–Ω –ò–ò (conf=62%) ‚Äî —ç–∫–æ–Ω–æ–º–∏–∫–∞ –∑–∞—â–∏—â–µ–Ω–∞");
2125
2126    println!("\n‚ïî‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïó");
2127    println!("‚ïë  ‚úÖ Mint Patch COMPLETE ‚Äî Adaptive Emission —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç        ‚ïë");
2128    println!("‚ïë                                                              ‚ïë");
2129    println!("‚ïë  EmissionPolicy ‚úì  IdeaLabSignal ‚úì  Cooldown ‚úì            ‚ïë");

2131    println!("‚ïë  DAO –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–∞–≥–∞–µ—Ç ‚Üí –ò–ò –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ—Ç ‚Üí —ç–∫–æ–Ω–æ–º–∏–∫–∞ –º–µ–Ω—è–µ—Ç—Å—è. ‚úì    ‚ïë");
2132    println!("‚ïö‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïù\n");
2133}

2136pub async fn run_crypto_demo() {
2137    use crate::chacha::{ChaCha20, ChaCha20Poly1305, X25519, FederationCipher};
2138
2139    println!("\n‚ïî‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïó");
2140    println!("‚ïë         FEDERATION CORE ‚Äî Phase 9 / Crypto Core             ‚ïë");
2141    println!("‚ïë         ChaCha20-Poly1305 + X25519  üîê                      ‚ïë");
2142    println!("‚ïö‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïù\n");
2143
2144    // ‚îÄ‚îÄ 1. ChaCha20 –ø–æ—Ç–æ–∫–æ–≤—ã–π —à–∏—Ñ—Ä ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
2145    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
2146    println!("  1. ChaCha20 ‚Äî –ø–æ—Ç–æ–∫–æ–≤—ã–π —à–∏—Ñ—Ä (RFC 8439)");
2147    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
2148
2149    let key: [u8;32] = [
2150        0x00,0x01,0x02,0x03,0x04,0x05,0x06,0x07,
2151        0x08,0x09,0x0a,0x0b,0x0c,0x0d,0x0e,0x0f,
2152        0x10,0x11,0x12,0x13,0x14,0x15,0x16,0x17,
2153        0x18,0x19,0x1a,0x1b,0x1c,0x1d,0x1e,0x1f,
2154    ];
2155    let nonce: [u8;12] = [0x00,0x00,0x00,0x00,
2156                           0x00,0x00,0x00,0x4a,
2157                           0x00,0x00,0x00,0x00];
2158
2159    let plaintext = b"PULSE:id=42,tactic=Aiki,nodes=2514,region=CN";
2160    let mut enc = ChaCha20::new(&key, &nonce, 1);
2161    let ciphertext = enc.encrypt(plaintext);
2162    let mut dec = ChaCha20::new(&key, &nonce, 1);
2163    let decrypted = dec.decrypt(&ciphertext);
2164
2165    println!("   –û—Ç–∫—Ä—ã—Ç—ã–π —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç: {}", std::str::from_utf8(plaintext).unwrap());
2166    print!("   –®–∏—Ñ—Ä—Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç:      ");
2167    for b in &ciphertext[..16] { print!("{:02x}", b); }
2168    println!("... ({} –±–∞–π—Ç)", ciphertext.len());
2169    println!("   –†–∞—Å—à–∏—Ñ—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ:  {}", std::str::from_utf8(&decrypted).unwrap());
2170    println!("   –°–æ–≤–ø–∞–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ:    {}", if plaintext == decrypted.as_slice() {"‚úÖ"} else {"‚ùå"});
2171
2172    // ‚îÄ‚îÄ 2. AEAD ChaCha20-Poly1305 ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
2173    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
2174    println!("  2. ChaCha20-Poly1305 AEAD (RFC 8439)");
2175    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
2176
2177    let aead = ChaCha20Poly1305::new(key);
2178    let message = b"PULSE:id=42,tactic=Aiki,nodes=2514";
2179    let aad = b"federation-core-v1";
2180
2181    let sealed = aead.seal(message, aad, &nonce);
2182    print!("   Nonce:    ");
2183    for b in &sealed.nonce { print!("{:02x}", b); }
2184    println!();
2185    print!("   Tag:      ");
2186    for b in &sealed.tag { print!("{:02x}", b); }
2187    println!();
2188    println!("   Payload:  {} ‚Üí {} –±–∞–π—Ç (+{} overhead)",
2189        message.len(), sealed.len(), sealed.len() - message.len());
2190
2191    match aead.open(&sealed, aad) {
2192        Ok(pt) => println!("   –í—Å–∫—Ä—ã—Ç–∏–µ: ‚úÖ \"{}\"", std::str::from_utf8(&pt).unwrap()),
2193        Err(e) => println!("   –í—Å–∫—Ä—ã—Ç–∏–µ: ‚ùå {}", e),
2194    }
2195
2196    // –¢–µ—Å—Ç –Ω–∞ –º–æ–¥–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—é ‚Äî –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–æ —É–ø–∞—Å—Ç—å
2197    let mut tampered = sealed.clone();
2198    tampered.ciphertext[0] ^= 0xff;
2199    match aead.open(&tampered, aad) {
2200        Ok(_)  => println!("   –ê—Ç–∞–∫–∞:    ‚ùå –ù–ï –û–ë–ù–ê–†–£–ñ–ï–ù–ê (–ø–ª–æ—Ö–æ)"),
2201        Err(e) => println!("   –ê—Ç–∞–∫–∞:    ‚úÖ –û–ë–ù–ê–†–£–ñ–ï–ù–ê ‚Äî \"{}\"", e),
2202    }
2203
2204    // ‚îÄ‚îÄ 3. X25519 ECDH ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
2205    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
2206    println!("  3. X25519 ‚Äî ECDH –æ–±–º–µ–Ω –∫–ª—é—á–∞–º–∏");
2207    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
2208
2209    let mut alice_x = X25519::new(0xA11C_E5EE_D000_0000u64);
2210    let mut bob_x   = X25519::new(0xB0B5_EED0_0000_0000u64);
2211
2212    let (alice_priv, alice_pub) = alice_x.generate_keypair();
2213    let (bob_priv,   bob_pub)   = bob_x.generate_keypair();
2214
2215    let alice_shared = X25519::diffie_hellman(&alice_priv, &bob_pub);
2216    let bob_shared   = X25519::diffie_hellman(&bob_priv,   &alice_pub);
2217
2218    print!("   Alice pub: ");
2219    for b in &alice_pub[..8] { print!("{:02x}", b); }
2220    println!("...");
2221    print!("   Bob pub:   ");
2222    for b in &bob_pub[..8] { print!("{:02x}", b); }
2223    println!("...");
2224    print!("   Alice shared: ");
2225    for b in &alice_shared[..8] { print!("{:02x}", b); }
2226    println!("...");
2227    print!("   Bob shared:   ");
2228    for b in &bob_shared[..8] { print!("{:02x}", b); }
2229    println!("...");
2230    println!("   –°–æ–≤–ø–∞–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ:   {}", if alice_shared == bob_shared {"‚úÖ"} else {"‚ùå"});
2231
2232    // ‚îÄ‚îÄ 4. FederationCipher ‚Äî –ø–æ–ª–Ω—ã–π –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–æ–∫–æ–ª ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
2233    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
2234    println!("  4. FederationCipher ‚Äî –∑–∞—à–∏—Ñ—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ Pulse");
2235    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
2236
2237    let mut cipher = FederationCipher::new();
2238    // –£—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞–≤–ª–∏–≤–∞–µ–º —Å–µ—Å—Å–∏–∏ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ shared secret
2239    cipher.establish_session("hub-berlin-01", &alice_shared);
2240    cipher.establish_session("hub-tokyo-01",  &bob_shared);
2241
2242    let pulses = vec![
2243        ("hub-berlin-01", "PULSE:id=1,tactic=AikiReflection,bypass=0.87,region=RU"),
2244        ("hub-tokyo-01",  "PULSE:id=2,tactic=CumulativeStrike,bypass=0.43,region=KP"),
2245        ("hub-berlin-01", "PULSE:id=3,tactic=Hybrid,nodes=2514,treasury=890.5"),
2246    ];
2247
2248    println!("   {:15}  {:>8}  {:>8}  {:>6}  –°—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å", "–ü–∏—Ä", "–û—Ç–∫—Ä—ã—Ç", "–ó–∞—à–∏—Ñ—Ä", "–û–≤–µ—Ä—Ö–µ–¥");
2249    println!("   {}", "‚îÄ".repeat(60));
2250
2251    for (peer, pulse) in &pulses {
2252        let aad = format!("aad:peer={}", peer);
2253        if let Some(ct) = cipher.encrypt_pulse(peer, pulse.as_bytes(), aad.as_bytes()) {
2254            let overhead = ct.len() - pulse.len();
2255            match cipher.decrypt_pulse(peer, &ct, aad.as_bytes()) {
2256                Ok(pt) => {
2257                    let ok = pt == pulse.as_bytes();
2258                    println!("   {:15}  {:>7}–±  {:>7}–±  {:>5}–±  {}",
2259                        peer, pulse.len(), ct.len(), overhead,
2260                        if ok {"‚úÖ OK"} else {"‚ùå MISMATCH"});
2261                }
2262                Err(e) => println!("   {:15}  ‚ùå {}", peer, e),
2263            }
2264        }
2265    }
2266
2267    // –¢–µ—Å—Ç: –Ω–µ–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª—å–Ω—ã–π AAD ‚Äî –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–æ —É–ø–∞—Å—Ç—å
2268    let ct = cipher.encrypt_pulse("hub-berlin-01",
2269        b"SECRET", b"correct-aad").unwrap();
2270    match cipher.decrypt_pulse("hub-berlin-01", &ct, b"wrong-aad") {
2271        Ok(_)  => println!("\n   AAD –∞—Ç–∞–∫–∞: ‚ùå –ù–ï –û–ë–ù–ê–†–£–ñ–ï–ù–ê"),
2272        Err(e) => println!("\n   AAD –∞—Ç–∞–∫–∞: ‚úÖ –û–ë–ù–ê–†–£–ñ–ï–ù–ê ‚Äî \"{}\"", e),
2273    }
2274
2275    let s = cipher.stats();
2276    println!("\n   –°–µ—Å—Å–∏–π: {}  –ó–∞—à–∏—Ñ—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ: {}  –†–∞—Å—à–∏—Ñ—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ: {}  –ë–∞–π—Ç: {}  AuthFail: {}",
2277        s.sessions, s.encrypt_count, s.decrypt_count,
2278        s.bytes_encrypted, s.auth_failures);
2279
2280    println!("\n‚ïî‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïó");
2281    println!("‚ïë  ‚úÖ Phase 9 COMPLETE ‚Äî Crypto Core —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç                 ‚ïë");
2282    println!("‚ïë                                                              ‚ïë");
2283    println!("‚ïë  ChaCha20 ‚úì  Poly1305 ‚úì  AEAD ‚úì  X25519 ‚úì                ‚ïë");
2284    println!("‚ïë  FederationCipher ‚úì  Tamper detection ‚úì  AAD guard ‚úì      ‚ïë");
2285    println!("‚ïë  –í—Å–µ Pulse –∑–∞—à–∏—Ñ—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω—ã. –¶–µ–Ω–∑–æ—Ä –≤–∏–¥–∏—Ç —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —à—É–º. ‚úì        ‚ïë");
2286    println!("‚ïö‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïù\n");

2327    let mut sim = WarSimulator::new();
2328

2330
2331    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");

2333        "–¢–∏–∫", "–§–∞–∑–∞", "–ñ–∏–≤—ã—Ö", "Inet", "Mesh", "Aiki", "Bypass", "Connct");
2334    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");

2336    sim.run_full();
2337
2338    // –í—ã–≤–æ–¥–∏–º –∫–ª—é—á–µ–≤—ã–µ —Ç–∏–∫–∏
2339    let key_ticks: Vec<usize> = (0..sim.history.len())
2340        .filter(|&i| {
2341            let t = sim.history[i].tick;
2342            t <= ATTACK_TICK + 1
2343                || t.is_multiple_of(5)
2344                || sim.history[i].phase != sim.history[i.saturating_sub(1)].phase
2345        })
2346        .collect();
2347
2348    let mut prev_phase = WarPhase::Peace;
2349    for &i in &key_ticks {
2350        let s = &sim.history[i];
2351        let phase_marker = if s.phase != prev_phase {
2352            prev_phase = s.phase.clone();
2353            format!(" {}", s.phase.icon())
2354        } else { "  ".to_string() };
2355
2356        let bypass_color = if s.bypass_rate_avg > 0.70 { "\x1b[32m" }
2357            else if s.bypass_rate_avg > 0.40 { "\x1b[33m" } else { "\x1b[31m" };
2358        let conn_color = if s.connectivity > 0.50 { "\x1b[32m" }
2359            else if s.connectivity > 0.25 { "\x1b[33m" } else { "\x1b[31m" };
2360
2361        println!("  {:>4}  {}{:10}\x1b[0m{}  {:>5}  {:>5}  {:>5}  {:>5}  \

2371            bypass_color, s.bypass_rate_avg * 100.0,
2372            conn_color, s.connectivity * 100.0,
2373            s.censor_exhaustion * 100.0, s.censor_resources * 100.0);
2374    }
2375
2376    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");

2380    println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
2381    println!("  –ò—Ç–æ–≥–∏ –≤–æ–π–Ω—ã");
2382    println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
2383    println!("  –§–∏–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ:");
2384    println!("  –ñ–∏–≤—ã—Ö —É–∑–ª–æ–≤:     {}/{}  ({:.1}%)",

2386        final_s.alive_nodes as f64 / WAR_NODES as f64 * 100.0);
2387    println!("  –°–≤—è–∑–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å —Å–µ—Ç–∏:  {:.1}%", final_s.connectivity * 100.0);
2388    println!("  Bypass rate:     {:.1}%", final_s.bypass_rate_avg * 100.0);

2390    println!("  –¶–µ–Ω–∑–æ—Ä –∏—Å—Ç–æ—â—ë–Ω:  {:.1}%  —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–æ–≤: {:.1}%",
2391        final_s.censor_exhaustion * 100.0, final_s.censor_resources * 100.0);
2392

2465        0xEC05_C0E5_EED0_0001u64,
2466        0xE905_EFEE_5EED_0002u64,

2468        0xBE01_B04E_ED00_0004u64,
2469        init_payload, resp_payload, final_payload,
2470    ) {
2471        Ok((mut init_sess, mut resp_sess, log)) => {
2472            println!("  –ö–ª—é—á–∏:");
2473            print!("  nexus-core-01 static pub: ");
2474            for b in &log.init_static_pub[..8] { print!("{:02x}", b); }

2478            println!("...\n");
2479

2481            println!("  ‚Üí msg1 (e):           {} –±–∞–π—Ç  payload: \"{}\"",
2482                log.msg1_len,

2484            println!("  ‚Üê msg2 (e,ee,s,es):   {} –±–∞–π—Ç  payload: \"{}\"",
2485                log.msg2_len,
2486                std::str::from_utf8(&log.msg2_payload).unwrap_or("?"));
2487            println!("  ‚Üí msg3 (s,se):        {} –±–∞–π—Ç  payload: \"{}\"",
2488                log.msg3_len,
2489                std::str::from_utf8(&log.msg3_payload).unwrap_or("?"));
2490
2491            println!("\n  Handshake hash:");
2492            print!("  nexus: ");
2493            for b in &log.handshake_hash[..16] { print!("{:02x}", b); }
2494            println!("...");
2495            println!("  –°–æ–≤–ø–∞–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ: {}", if log.hashes_match {"‚úÖ"} else {"‚ùå"});
2496
2497            println!("\n‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ");
2498            println!("  –¢—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ —Ö–µ–Ω–¥—à–µ–π–∫–∞");
2499            println!("‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ\n");
2500
2501            let pulses = vec![
2502                "PULSE:id=1,tactic=AikiReflection,bypass=0.87,region=CN",
2503                "PULSE:id=2,nodes=2514,treasury=24891.3",
2504                "PULSE:id=3,event=halving_imminent,blocks=47291",
2505            ];
2506
2507            for pulse in &pulses {
2508                let ct = init_sess.send(pulse.as_bytes());
2509                match resp_sess.recv(&ct) {
2510                    Ok(pt) => {
2511                        let ok = pt == pulse.as_bytes();
2512                        println!("  nexus ‚Üí berlin: {}–± ‚Üí {}–±  {}  \"{}\"",
2513                            pulse.len(), ct.len(),
2514                            if ok {"‚úÖ"} else {"‚ùå"},
2515                            std::str::from_utf8(&pt).unwrap_or("?"));
2516                    }
2517                    Err(e) => println!("  ‚ùå {}", e),
2518                }
2519            }
2520
2521            // –û–±—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω—ã–π –∫–∞–Ω–∞–ª
2522            let reply = b"ACK:hub-berlin-01,trust=0.977,mesh_nodes=334";
2523            let ct = resp_sess.send(reply);
2524            match init_sess.recv(&ct) {
2525                Ok(pt) => println!("\n  berlin ‚Üí nexus: {}–± ‚Üí {}–±  ‚úÖ  \"{}\"",
2526                    reply.len(), ct.len(),
2527                    std::str::from_utf8(&pt).unwrap_or("?")),
2528                Err(e) => println!("  ‚ùå {}", e),
2529            }
2530
2531            // –ê—Ç–∞–∫–∞: replay —Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å–µ–≥–æ —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏—è
2532            let stale_ct = init_sess.send(b"FAKE_REPLAY");
2533            match resp_sess.recv(&stale_ct) {
2534                Ok(_)  => println!("\n  Replay –∞—Ç–∞–∫–∞: ‚ùå –ù–ï –û–ë–ù–ê–†–£–ñ–ï–ù–ê"),
2535                Err(e) => println!("\n  Replay –∞—Ç–∞–∫–∞: ‚úÖ –û–ë–ù–ê–†–£–ñ–ï–ù–ê ‚Äî \"{}\"", e),
2536            }
2537
2538            let s = init_sess.messages_sent + resp_sess.messages_sent;
2539            let b = init_sess.bytes_sent + resp_sess.bytes_sent;
2540            println!("\n  Channel binding: {:02x?}", init_sess.channel_binding());
2541            println!("  –°–µ—Å—Å–∏—è: —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–π={} –±–∞–π—Ç={}", s, b);
2542        }
2543        Err(e) => println!("  ‚ùå Handshake failed: {}", e),
2544    }
2545
2546    println!("\n‚ïî‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïó");
2547    println!("‚ïë  ‚úÖ Noise Protocol XX COMPLETE                              ‚ïë");
2548    println!("‚ïë                                                              ‚ïë");
2549    println!("‚ïë  SymmetricState ‚úì  CipherState ‚úì  HandshakeState ‚úì        ‚ïë");

2552    println!("‚ïö‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïù\n");

2576        
2577        // –§–∞–∑–∞ 3: –§–µ–¥–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è –∞–¥–∞–ø—Ç–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç—Å—è
2578        let p3 = sim.run_phase("Phase 3: Federation Adapts", 20, 6);
2579        println!("üõ°Ô∏è  Phase 3: {} - Delivery: {:.1}%", p3.phase_name, p3.delivery_rate * 100.0);
2580        println!("    Censor: {} (CPU: {:.0}%)", p3.censor_status, p3.censor_cpu * 100.0);
2581        println!("    Strategy: {}", p3.censor_strategy);
2582        
2583        println!("\n‚úÖ –ë–∏—Ç–≤–∞ –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–∞!");
2584        println!("Final delivery: {:.1}%", p3.delivery_rate * 100.0);
2585        
2586        assert!(p3.delivery_rate > 0.3, "–§–µ–¥–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–∞ –≤—ã–∂–∏—Ç—å!");
2587    }
2588}
